< review>
First off it's not the same Pho Star restaurant that I use to eat at since 2016. I would have to say that the name of the restaurant stayed the same. But it's not the same owner nor the same food for the same employees working there. I used to eat there a lot when they first opened in that location and I knew the owner and all of the employees.  I really enjoyed the service and the food there before. I can tell that their menu changed as well as the service. The service wasn't that great it took longer to be seated for a smaller restaurant, the service and the courteous  of the employees wasn't great like it used to be. Why because the service took longer  then the previous owners and employees that used to work there. The foods not the same. They also served me a type of an orange like Boba with a fruity liquid Center which made the Thai tea taste different. They did not use the original black chewy tapioca Boba that's usually served in most bobas today. I was unhappy with my drink for I was expecting the Boba that I used to purchase when I used to go to the Pho Star. I had asked the owner why they serve the Thai tea with that type of boba in it letting me employee know that this is not the way I have ever purchased a Thai tea boba his explanation was that they were out of the tapioca balls and if they were out of tapioca balls he should have came back to the table and explain to me that they were out instead of replacing it with a fruity liquidy boba served in the Thai tea. I usually order the brisket steak pho soup as I noticed that has changed as well it didn't taste the same as it wasn't served the same. All I have to say now is that I will probably be looking for a new for a restaurant to be eating at for I was not pleased with the experience either the new ownership change over as well as a service.</review>

<Rate>1<//Rate><text>I wanted to like this place. It is super close to my house I could walk here.

I started with egg rolls, they were mushy and tasted worse than frozen and then microwaved egg rolls.

There were no plates for sauces at our table, and our server had to check three tables to find some. He brought over three plates, two of the three were dirty. My fiance went to pour some soy sauce so she could dip her egg rolls and try to make them edible and the plastic bottle was plugged shut with old sauce. She had to clear it with a fork and poured the crusty bits into one of the dirty dishes we were brought.
.
The broth spoons at our table were dirty.

I ordered Pho the broth was ok, and that's being kind.  There was more fat than meat in my bowl, and the little bit of meat I got was very tough and not very good. I only could eat a few bites before I lost my appetite, and I am not a picky eater.

I was looking forward to a good dinner, and I was very let down. I often enjoy Pho, and I have never been to such a bad place. The lack of customers, and that someone was passed out sleeping in the BMW M4 that was parked outside crooked in two spots next to the front door should have been a sign.

I noticed that they are under new management, so I am not sure if the positive reviews were from previous management/owners, but I would be shocked if others had a positive experience here.

I left my uneaten food on the table, paid the tab and left. I would have felt bad and awkward refusing to pay for my food even though it was horrible. I will not be back. I ended up going home and cooking my own dinner. Save your money and appetite, visit somewhere else.</text><Pics>None</Pics>< response>

<time>1607382954129</time><Rating>5<//Rating>< Text>
Wow!  What a find!  I had the Chicken and Avocado Salad on Sweet Potato Toast (which was simply a slice of sweet potato.   It was one of the best meals I've had in ages. So tasty!  I Asiago had the seasonal Vegis which was mostly caramelized carrots, onions a little mushroom and a little pepper (like a bell pepper, but maybe a red pepper).  Perfectly caramelized!  I finished with a "paleo" brownie.  So soft, warm,  just the right amount of gooeyness.   It was had a carmalized maple chocolate flavor. A little sweet for me... but maybe that's good l.  If it has been less sweet I would have eaten the whole thing.  As it was a only had a few bites and was then completely satisfied.  Milk would have been a good addition for me to help wash it down. They do serve grass fed milk,  I just didn't get it.  I highly recommend this place.  Its pricey for me but the quality and taste justifies the price.< /Text>

<review>We have been ordering Rosemary's delivery for almost a month now and can't say enough good stuff about it. The food is delicious - both my wife and I are foodies and we have yet to find a meal we haven't liked.

The portions are awesome too (coming from a 6'5" 250 lb dude), i never finish a meal wishing I had more - just right.

Their customer service is even better, any issue we have had have been promptly and excellently solved. Heck - Rose even made a delivery herself when we ran into an issue on a drop off.

The meals come in  a recyclable container that are ready to pop in the oven. Just take the lid off - put in at 375 and 12-15 minute later - boom - awesome home cooked meal with tons of flavor and on our meal plan.

Seriously - Rosemary's have given my wife and I our evenings back. No more worrying over who's cooking dinner or having to break and order take-out off plan.

The only real problem is we had to stop ordering the brownies because they were so good we'd eat 4 (they are HUGE!) in just a couple days.

Delicious, nutritious, affordable, and easy. What more could you ask for?< /review><GmapID>0x808525c7bca95275:0xfee18af5bc2e537b</GmapID><UserId.>117663441348192196186< /UserId.><Time>1573701131698<//Time><pics>None< /pics><user_name>Sev Johnson< /user_name>< Resp>

<text>My wife and I ordered some candy from here as a reward to ourselves after she had been following a very regimented diet and after the stresses of moving into a new place and starting a new job. We had heard really good things about this candy, so we were hoping it was going to be delicious.

<review>6/6/13

LITTLE HELP, PLEASE?

I drove in to Sunny Acres but wasn't sure I had found the correct street address as it wasn't clearly marked from the main road. Luckily I saw an "office" sign in front of me and parked there. The way I see it, you get one lifetime to be the best person you can be. To make life for others as great as possible, and to enjoy it yourself. I just don't understand it when I come across people who are unkind, and in this case, unfriendly!

<Name>John Smith<//Name>< review>
Was getting my tire fixed at discount tire, so I walked over here for lunch with a coworker looking for food.  Little hole in the wall Salvadorian place next to random stores, also doubles as a little bakery.

I got the Pupusa de chicharr√≥n y queso x2 and a Pupusa de frijol y queso. A Pupusa is a small salvadorian item that's essentially a fried tortilla with stuff inside it. The one I got had pork (chicharron) and queso (cheese), while the other one had frijol (beans) and queso. They're $1.50 each! Way cheap, since they're not too big, so I got three, which was a good portion for lunch. They were really tasty, and crunchy, and cheesy. Definitely a very homely place, and they also have a decent bit of other dishes and aguas frescas like horchata and fresh juices.

Cool little place.<//review>

I told him I did and provided my name for verification he then asked if the keys were in the vehicle and I told him yes.  I asked where the restroom was and he told me where it was.
